            <script type="b28677685969c06b8809f344-text/javascript">
                // Fungsi untuk mendapatkan nama hari
                function getDayName(dayIndex) {
                    const days = ["Min", "Sen", "Sel", "Rab", "Kam", "Jum", "Sab"];
                    return days[dayIndex] || "";
                }

                // Dapatkan elemen tanggal
                const dateElement = document.querySelector('[data-section="date"]');

                if (dateElement) {
                    const today = new Date();
                    const dayName = getDayName(today.getDay());
                    const dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, "0");
                    const mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0");
                    // bulan dimulai dari 0
                    const yy = String(today.getFullYear()).slice(-2);
                    // dua digit tahun
                    dateElement.textContent = `${dayName}, ${dd}/${mm}/${yy} - Toto 5 D`;
                }
            </script>
